BatterySwollen.c(26):                 <div class="col-lg-5 repair-bg-green repair-hero-txt-box">\n
BatterySwollen.c(26):                    <h1>Experiencing battery swelling?</h1>\n
BatterySwollen.c(26):     <p>If you have noticed that your notebook has a slight bulge or no longer sits flat, this 
BatterySwollen.c(26):     may indicate that your battery may be swollen.</p>\n
BatterySwollen.c(26):     <p>Battery swelling is the result of the generation of gases per the normal degradation of
BatterySwollen.c(26):      the battery cell over time and does not present a safety issue. In order to protect your 
BatterySwollen.c(26):     hardware from potential damage, HP recommends that customers experiencing battery swelling
BatterySwollen.c(26):      discontinue use of the notebook until the battery can be replaced.</p>\n
BatterySwollen.c(26):     \n
BatterySwollen.c(26):                 </div>\n
BatterySwollen.c(26):              </div>\n

BatterySwollen.c(26):        </div>\n

BatterySwollen.c(26):     P battery is under warranty, HP will replace the battery per the terms and conditions of t
BatterySwollen.c(26):     he HP Worldwide Limited Warranty or applicable HP Care Packs. For batteries no longer unde
BatterySwollen.c(26):     r warranty, we can help you purchase a certified HP genuine replacement battery.</p>\n

BatterySwollen.c(158):                 <div class="col-lg-5 repair-bg-green repair-hero-txt-box">\n
BatterySwollen.c(158):                    <h1>Experiencing battery swelling?</h1>\n
BatterySwollen.c(158):     <p>If you have noticed that your notebook has a slight bulge or no longer sits flat, this 
BatterySwollen.c(158):     may indicate that your battery may be swollen.</p>\n
BatterySwollen.c(158):     <p>Battery swelling is the result of the generation of gases per the normal degradation of
BatterySwollen.c(158):      the battery cell over time and does not present a safety issue. In order to protect your 
BatterySwollen.c(158):     hardware from potential damage, HP recommends that customers experiencing battery swelling
BatterySwollen.c(158):      discontinue use of the notebook until the battery can be replaced.</p>\n
BatterySwollen.c(158):     \n
BatterySwollen.c(158):                 </div>\n
